China Navigation Cooperation: Board of Directors to be Established on May 1st

The Ministry of Transportation's approval response for the nationwide navigation cooperation has arrived. It has been decided to formally establish the organization ahead of schedule on May 1st. As this concerns the recovery of navigation rights and the realization of cooperation, the details will be published again as follows:

Cooperation Principles

This association is established in accordance with the concrete plan for China Navigation Cooperation approved by the Ministry of Transportation on December 29th, the 22nd year of the Republic (1933). The principles of this association are coexistence and co-prosperity, striving for navigation cooperation, protecting navigation routes, regulating supply and demand, and undertaking other cooperative matters as its mission. The office and joint business offices for each navigation route will be located in Shanghai. Branch offices and agencies may be established in other locations. The concrete cooperation plan is based on the minutes of previous meetings. Regarding water and land intermodal transportation, it is still based on the resolution of the joint meeting of the Ministry of Transportation and the Ministry of Railways, with civil aviation participating in the water and land intermodal transportation meeting.

Membership Qualifications

All Chinese-nationality shipping companies are eligible to be members. The cooperative matters agreed upon by members before the establishment of the cooperative shall be transferred to the association. Members have the responsibility to assist the association in carrying out various cooperative matters, abide by various resolutions, and bear various legitimate expenses. If three directors believe that a resolution of the members' meeting is difficult to implement, it can be decided by the board of directors, or the decision to approve or reject it will not be established. The standing director may submit it to the members' meeting at any time or submit it to the Ministry of Transportation for review.

Early Establishment

The cooperation plan has been submitted to the Ministry of Transportation for approval and record. The state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, based on the draft cooperation plan, sent a letter to the Shanghai Shipowners Association, requesting the rapid organization of the board of directors and requesting that the board of directors of the China Navigation Cooperative be formally organized and established on May 1st. Then, the board of directors will generate a secretariat, specialized committees, and joint operating offices for each route. After discussion by the Municipal Shipowners Association, it was decided to hold a board of directors election meeting next Monday at 2:00 PM. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will nominate five people, and the other private aviation representatives will nominate six people. The announcement has already been issued yesterday.

Recovering Navigation Rights

The China Navigation Cooperative is the foundation for recovering navigation rights. After the board of directors is established on May 1st, the first tasks to be handled are based on the investigation reports of the specialized committees: (1) adjusting the navigation routes of various routes in the Yangtze River and the sea; (2) balancing the supply and demand of cargo transportation based on tonnage and frequency; (3) realizing the unity and cooperation of state-owned and private aviation; (4) making everything public and permanently eliminating the deceptive and fraudulent fare reductions. Through spiritual cooperation, the aim is to gradually recover the lost navigation rights. This move by the navigation industry is truly an amazing feat, and the future of Chinese ships will be greatly illuminated.

Art Exhibition: Preview Day Fifteen

Yesterday (the 22nd) was the fifteenth day of the Shanghai preview of the London International Exhibition of Chinese Art. Yesterday was Monday, and as usual, visits were suspended in the morning, but the important staff of the association still went to the meeting to work as usual. In the afternoon, it was open as usual from 1:00 PM, and the number of visitors was still crowded, especially students from various schools, because group tickets could be used for admission in the afternoon on Mondays. Mr. Ye Gongchuo has also recently visited the meeting to view the art. Mr. Ye is a calligrapher and painter, so he feels a special and strong interest in calligraphy and painting. The calligraphy and painting exhibited by the association this time includes works by various artists. Some use meticulous brushwork, while others use bold brushwork. Generally, meticulous works are suitable for close viewing, while bold works are suitable for viewing from a distance, and naturally, there is endless interest. For example, the paintings of Wen Zhengming and Qiu Ying are suitable for close viewing. Every blade of grass, every tree, every house, every bridge, figures, mountains, and rivers are extremely meticulous. If you overlook them, it is difficult to appreciate their beauty. For example, Dong Yuan's "Dragon Dwelling Suburban People Picture" and Mi Fu's "Spring Mountain Auspicious Pine Picture" are suitable for viewing from a distance, and you will feel that the atmosphere is majestic, as if thousands of mountains and valleys are all in front of you, and you can appreciate the beauty of nature. Other items such as porcelain and bronze wares are suitable for carefully examining their patterns and quality, comparing the products of different eras. When viewing jade artifacts and cloisonné, you should have an artistic concept. Viewing archaeological examples can evoke memories of the lives of the people in the past. If you browse through these more than 900 antiques once, it will definitely increase your knowledge a lot. Chinese painting is very different from Western painting. Here is Chapter 4 of the "Characteristics of Chinese Painting" and its painting methods written by the association, which will be revealed below.

Characteristics and Painting Methods of Chinese Painting

The above two systems (referring to landscape, figure, and sketch systems) are only for those who specialize in each field. Often, one person is proficient in all three. There is no need to elaborate here. However, Chinese painting can almost completely express the personality, temperament, and interest of the author. This point is necessary for those who study Chinese painting to understand and acknowledge. The reasons for this are: (1) art and life are almost completely integrated; (2) painting methods are completely connected to calligraphy; (3) the tools used and the methods of using them are very subtle, so this result is formed. Chinese painting tools use brushes purely, and there are distinctions between thick and thin, hard and soft. Once a stroke is made, it is no longer changed. Therefore, the wrinkles and dyes in landscapes are different from piling up and decorating, and the strength and interest are contained within them. Although the yin and yang, facing and backing, and various proportions are not very strict, the general outline is not too far off, also because there is an aura that covers and reflects it. Also, when using ink and various colors, in addition to paying special attention to the methods of grinding, blending, and freezing, when using them, it is also due to the order of strokes, the lightness and heaviness of the force, the composition of water and various colors, and the combination of colors, as well as the interaction of the brush, paper (or silk), and color, resulting in brilliance and flavor, thus forming various functions. Therefore, when making paper, silk, pigments, brushes, and painting, special techniques are required for processing paper, silk, and pigments (such as wetting the paper first, mounting the silk first, and using a certain quality of water for mixing colors, etc.). Even the types of brushes are as many as thirty or forty kinds. It is also known to others that in addition to using paper and silk, there are those who paint on buildings and utensils, and there are those who use fingers, tongues, or brushes instead of brushes. In addition, there are fire paintings, iron paintings, paper weaving paintings, and flocked paintings, which should be listed in art and crafts. One more point should be clarified: Chinese painting has its own true face and spirit, but it has also been greatly influenced by foreign cultures throughout history. For example, the transmission of Buddhism, the communication of envoys, and the import of goods and industrial products have all greatly impacted the style of painting, but most of them can be chewed and melted, forming a work with a national color. Therefore, China must be regarded as a giant in the world's painting schools. (There is also a chapter on the outline of the calligraphy and painting exhibits this time, which will be published tomorrow.)

Chairman's Report: The assembly publicly elected Liu Zhongying as chairman, Ge Futian as master of ceremonies, and Xu Chengde as recorder. After the ceremony, Chairman Liu Zhongying reported, stating that last year, there was no rain in eastern Zhejiang for several months, and the fields were cracked. It was truly a thousand miles of red land, and the crops were not harvested. The misery of the general disaster victims, crying from hunger and cold, was truly heartbreaking. The hope for the development of our national goods industry originally lies in the countryside, because it is impossible to talk about promoting national goods in this civilized city full of foreign influence. Therefore, if we in the national goods industry need to seek the development of our own future, we must first come to the rescue of the countryside. If the countryside does not recover, national goods will never be able to thrive. If we want to recover the countryside, we should first provide relief to the disaster victims. If we want to provide relief to the disaster victims, we should ask everyone to pay attention to the mission initiated by this association. Now that we have all sponsored and participated, we must earnestly maintain this "Shanghai National Goods Movement Aid Relief Fair" and enable it to achieve excellent results in the end.

Resolutions: The resolutions are as follows: (A) The opening date of the assembly is set for the 26th of this month. Please ratify the public decision. Resolution: Passed. (B) The assembly will have an attached amusement section. Each amusement ticket will cost three cents. Participating manufacturers will receive tickets from the assembly and give them to guests with their goods during business hours. The income from the tickets will be used for disaster relief. Please pass the public decision. Resolution: (1) One cent of the ticket price will be used for amusement expenses, and two cents will be used for disaster relief. (2) The amusement tickets will be issued by the Jiaxu Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association, which will send staff to be stationed at the assembly to sell them. (C) The invoices for the temporary market should be stipulated to be printed and issued by the assembly to show uniformity. Each book will cost two dimes. Please pass the resolution. Resolution: Passed. (D) The staff of the assembly and the employees of each manufacturer should wear badges to show identification. Resolution: Passed. (E) The opening ceremony of the assembly and the list of officials. Please pass the public decision. (The list is recorded separately). Resolution: Passed. (F) How should the assembly's fire protection and emergency preparedness be set up? Resolution: Send a letter to the Fire Brigade and the Public Security Bureau to send a team to prevent it. (G) Issue a declaration. Resolution: Hand it over to Le Qin, the secretary general of the assembly, to draft.

Temporary Motion: The assembly's funding is insufficient, and most of the participating manufacturers' booth fees are paid with post-dated checks, while the construction costs and the deposit for connecting electricity are very high. How should this be handled? Resolution: Instruct each manufacturer to cash in their checks to maintain the assembly.

The association previously sent representatives to Beijing to petition the Ministry of Finance, but the results were not satisfactory. Therefore, in order to quickly realize its plan, it was decided to send representatives to Beijing again to petition again. The selection of representatives and the date of going to Beijing will be determined soon. The draft of the petition, which is thousands of words long, has also been drafted. The benefits of the property circulation vouchers and the methods of raising them are described in detail in the petition.

Financial Community Observation

Yesterday's meeting of the association was extremely secret, and attendance certificates were attached to the notices distributed before the meeting. According to observations by financial giants in this port, the issuance of these property circulation vouchers will definitely not be realized. The reason is very obvious. The issuance of property circulation vouchers is naturally the same as the issuance of banknotes by banks. The issuance of 450 million yuan of property circulation vouchers must have a 60% cash guarantee in order to be trusted. Otherwise, relying solely on the numbers of the property circulation vouchers, not only will people from all walks of life not trust them, but even the issuers of the association will be half-believing and half-doubting each other and unable to bear it. The cash guarantee for the issuance of 450 million yuan of circulation vouchers is 270 million yuan. The silver deposits in various banks in Shanghai are currently only 30 to 40 million yuan. Where will the 270 million yuan be raised from? The current panic in the market and the decline of all industries are also due to the lack of cash. If 470 million yuan can be raised to be used as a cash guarantee for property circulation vouchers, then the issuance of property circulation vouchers would be a superfluous act.

Entomologist Zhang Juebo Talks About Plant Disease Inspection Our Country's Insect Pest Losses Reach 400 Million Annually

The famous entomologist Zhang Juebo, director of the Zhejiang Entomology Bureau, came to Shanghai on official business a few days ago. A reporter from the National Society specially visited him and asked Mr. Zhang's opinions on plant disease and insect pest inspection. According to him, in recent years, countries around the world have attached great importance to the prevention and control of plant diseases and insect pests. On the one hand, they painstakingly study and eliminate methods and provide practical guidance to farmers. On the other hand, they formulate inspection regulations and implement the inspection of imported and exported plants. The handling is meticulous and the results are remarkable. The direct suppression of the danger of disease and insects at its inception, and the indirect establishment of the guarantee of plant production, its significance is self-evident. However, the inherent diseases and insects in our country have become extremely serious problems that need to be solved urgently.

Annual Losses

The annual losses are always more than 400 million yuan, which is almost six times the annual income of the central government. However, the plants imported from abroad are still not inspected and are freely transported and sold without limit. As a result, the dangerous insects and bacteria from abroad enter at every opportunity. For example, the red bollworm, the cotton scale insect, and the wheat smut disease were all transmitted from overseas and have become quite widespread in recent years, almost everywhere. The harm is so great that it is beyond the imagination of ordinary people. As for the insects and bacteria that have not been imported but have the possibility of being imported, they are also cause for concern. Take the cotton boll weevil and the cabbage clubroot disease as examples. They are extremely rampant in the United States, and farmers suffer great losses. If they are unfortunately transmitted to our country, the future of cotton and vegetable business will be unthinkable. There is also something that cannot be said enough, that is, the severity of diseases and pests imported from other places often exceeds that of the place of origin. This is because the environments of various countries are different and the climates are different. The insects and bacteria in the place of origin are often subject to the restraint of natural enemies and climate, or because the resistance of the host in the local area is strong and cannot be rampant. Once transmitted to a foreign country, the natural balance is lost, and it often leads to major disasters. For example, the grape mildew transmitted from France to the United States and the citrus scale insect transmitted from China to the United States are all clear examples. However, this is only in terms of preventing insects and bacteria from abroad.

Necessity of Inspection

In terms of foreign trade, our country's exported plants have always had no legal authority to inspect and prove the losses suffered over the years, which is even more alarming. Because our farmers are ignorant of the procedures for preventing and controlling diseases and insect pests, the exported plants often carry dangerous insects and bacteria. Some are completely burned by foreign inspectors, and some are ordered to return to the place of origin. Some even prohibit the import of Chinese plants and plant products directly in order to prevent the spread of diseases and insect pests. This is also an important reason for the sluggishness of our country's foreign trade. It is recently heard that the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry has launched plant disease and insect pest inspection, which is an essential plan for both the country and the world, which cannot be ignored. I deeply hope that people from all walks of life will not regard it as an ordinary problem and ignore it.

Through Chongming and Hai'an Ships: Prohibition of Sampans Picking Up Passengers, Implemented from the First Day of Next Month

The Shanghai-based Ping An, Da Xing, Ju Feng, Da Da, and other companies operating ships to Chongming and Hai'an, due to repeated incidents of sampans vying for passengers, resulting in capsizing and drowning deaths, have now decided that from May 1st, the five ships on the Chongming and Hai'an routes will prohibit sampan passenger pick-up. They have requested the magistrates of the counties of Chongming and Hai'an to issue strict prohibitions. The details are as follows:

Lingdian Port Tragedy

The sampan operators in Lingdian Port are exceptionally aggressive, disregarding prohibitions. Last month, sampans competing for passengers led to a full boat capsizing, resulting in the tragic drowning of a large number of passengers. Afterwards, the government and party organizations of the county, together with the five shipping companies, carefully discussed how to handle the aftermath, and are addressing the bereaved families of the deceased.

Sampans Prohibited from Picking Up Passengers

Ping An, Da Xing, Ju Feng, Da Da, and the other five shipping companies, after discussing with the government and party organizations, decided that for future voyages to Chongming and Hai'an, in order to prevent sampan tragedies and safeguard the lives of passengers, it is essential to strictly prohibit the sampan operators at each port from forcibly approaching the ships and competing for passengers. Starting from May 1st, the five shipping companies will uniformly notify each ship to prohibit opening the gangway doors, not allowing sampans to forcibly approach, and requesting the Jinghai naval vessels to strictly investigate and prohibit. If any sampan operators forcibly solicit passengers, they will be immediately detained and dealt with. The companies are also requesting the county magistrates to issue public announcements so that passengers disembark and embark using the ship's large rowing boats.

Requesting County Magistrates to Issue Public Announcements

The five companies sent a special letter to the magistrates of the counties of Chongming and Hai'an, stating that the sampan operators at each port compete for passengers, disregarding the load capacity, causing repeated capsizing. Although many port authorities have complied with previous prohibitions, for the past year, there have also been many who have disregarded the prohibitions. Such as the recent tragic sampan capsize in Lingdian Port, which is due to the aggressive nature of the sampan operators there. The case is still in the process of convening both sides to negotiate a settlement, and it is also planned to order the shipping companies to instruct their crew members not to allow sampans to approach again. If there is any further violation, the crew members should bear full responsibility, etc. Since the government and party organizations aim to ensure passenger safety and incorporate operations into a regular business, the prohibition of sampans competing for passengers should be complied with. However, the sampan operators are exceptionally unreasonable and cannot be reasoned with through words. It is indeed necessary, in addition to the company notifying each ship that starting from May 1st, the gangway doors will not be opened to prohibit sampans from approaching, to request the county government to issue a public announcement of the implementation date, so that passengers will no longer be deceived by sampan operators. If passengers still mistakenly take sampans, resulting in risks, the port police and Jinghai naval vessels should investigate and prohibit it at any time.

Dozens of Pounds of Large Bomb Explodes: Five Dead, Nine Injured. Trying to Catch Fresh Fish Fails, Instead, a Large Bomb is Discovered. First Throw Does Not Explode, Second Throw Booms and Explodes, Causing this Tragedy.

Yesterday evening at approximately 7:30, near the Dongyue Temple in Jiangwan, a bomb explosion occurred, killing five people and injuring nine. The following is a narrative of the incident. A man named Wang Xiaoquan from Haimen, 22 years old, residing at No. 87 Wan'an Road in Jiangwan, usually worked pulling a small cart. Yesterday evening around 5:00 PM, after Wang Xiaoquan returned home from pulling his cart, feeling tired from the day's work and lacking any side dishes for his wine, he took a basket alone to the riverbank there to catch fresh fish. Unexpectedly, instead of catching fish, he discovered a bomb, over two feet long and weighing dozens of pounds. At that time, Wang Xiaoquan did not know what it was and happily took it home, showing it to his family and neighbors. More than ten people gathered to watch, but several of them recognized it as a bomb and quickly told him what it was. However, Wang Xiaoquan paid no attention and even threw the bomb. The first attempt did not cause it to explode, so he picked it up again and threw it forcefully. Unexpectedly, the bomb exploded, creating an earth-shattering boom. A cloud of smoke filled the air, and flesh and blood flew everywhere. Screams of pain followed. All fifteen bystanders suffered serious injuries. Fortunately, the police officer on duty at the Jiangwan branch quickly arrived after hearing the explosion and urgently telegraphed Branch Chief Dai Hongen, who personally led officers Li Qingxin, Patrol Officer Li Shuchen, Police Chiefs Zhang Huan, Wang Ruiying, Chen Yushan, and the entire team of police officers to the scene to investigate, maintain order, and notify the Zhabei and Jiangwan fire brigades to dispatch all ambulances to the scene to rescue the injured. After the firefighters carried out the injured one by one, it was discovered that four people had been killed instantly: Wang Xiaoquan (the instigator), whose hands and left foot had been blown off; Wang Li, 25 years old, from Jiangwan; Wang Gendi (female), 4 years old, from Jiangwan; and Cao Ximao, 4 years old, from Tongzhou. Another person, Hou Zhiqing, 59 years old, died of his injuries on the way to the hospital, so the total number of deaths was five. There were nine other seriously injured people: Wang Lianfang (male), 51 years old, from Jiangwan; Zhao Asan (male), 49 years old, from Jiangwan; Chen Zhaodi (female), 7 years old, from Haimen; Wang Chen (female), 27 years old, from Jiangwan; Chen Saner (male), 24 years old, from Haimen; Cao Lincai (male), 15 years old, from Jiangwan; Cao Zhu (female), 70 years old, from Haimen; Lu Wang (female), 30 years old, from Tongzhou; and Lu Wang (female), 63 years old, from Tongzhou. Branch Chief Dai Hongen personally escorted them to the Chinese Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road, the Binlong Hospital, and the New Zha Road Red Cross branch for treatment. However, because the injuries were severe, it is difficult to predict whether their lives can be saved. As for the five bodies killed by the bomb, Chief Dai ordered the local bailiff to request the court to examine them this morning, and also reported the situation to the headquarters. As for the site of the bomb explosion, a large hole was formed in the ground. Everyone in the vicinity heard the explosion, which shows the explosive power of the bomb. Considering its origin, it was likely left over from the war a few years ago. However, the ignorant people often do not know the dangers and treat them as toys, bringing them home at will, causing major disasters. This has happened frequently. Although it can be said that the disaster was self-inflicted, it is still tragic.

Campaign to Revoke Foreman's Permit: Lawsuit for Fraudulent Money: Claiming to Know a Staff Member of the Public Security Bureau and Parading it Around: Trial Opens Yesterday After Prosecutor's Indictment

The coal transportation work for the South City China Electric Company was previously contracted by Chen Defa and others. Now, a man named Ji Genfa has petitioned the Public Security Bureau to protect the transportation of coal for the China Electric Company and to revoke Chen Defa's permit as a shoulder-carrying foreman, etc. After the petition was approved, mediation was conducted first. There was a dispute at that time. Afterwards, Ji Genfa sued Chen Guansheng in the local court, accusing him of fraud for 400 yuan and requesting a thorough investigation. Prosecutor Ouyang Shu arrested Chen Guansheng, who confessed to the crime. He was indicted in the Criminal Court, stating that the defendant Chen Guansheng, claiming to know a staff member of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, Mr. Wang, had been boasting about it. On February 21st of this year, Li Genfa, a foreman for the North China Coal Company, because the company had recently signed a new coal purchase contract with the China Electric Company, wanted to have the permit of Chen Defa, the shoulder-carrying foreman used when the China Electric Company purchased coal from the Yitaixing Coal Company, revoked, and wanted to take over the job himself. He knew that this kind of wish would not easily be approved by the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, so he consulted Xia Liubao to ask Chen Guansheng, who promised to handle the matter for a handling fee of 400 yuan. Li Genfa borrowed 400 yuan from his relative Cai Guitang and, through Xue Dezhang and Li Yunqi, handed it to Chen Guansheng at the Lequn Inn on Wuma Road, Daxin Street, and obtained a receipt. On the next day, February 22nd, Li Genfa received a bureau notice ("Please wait for mediation"), realizing that he had been deceived. On February 25th of the same month, Li Genfa filed a lawsuit with the court against Chen Guansheng for fraud. The reasons for the indictment and the relevant articles of law are that Chen Guansheng admitted to receiving 400 yuan from Li Genfa and had repeatedly bribed Mr. Wang of the Public Security Bureau, but Mr. Wang refused to accept it. However, based on the testimony of witness Xia Liubao that Chen Guansheng wanted a handling fee of 400 yuan to get the permit, and the testimony of Li Genfa that Chen Guansheng wanted a deposit of 400 yuan, but after handing it over, there was no receipt on the approval, he knew he had been deceived, and the testimony of witness Li Lianqi that Chen Guansheng said he knew Mr. Wang and could guarantee the permit for a deposit of 400 yuan, it is sufficient to prove that Guansheng fraudulently obtained money. Chen Guansheng, intending to illegally possess it for himself, used deception to make others hand over their property, which is clearly a crime under Article 363, Paragraph 1. Yesterday morning, Judge Meng Tingke specially opened the Ninth Court to hear the case. First, the plaintiff Li Genfa testified that he was the transportation foreman at the North China Coal Company. When asked why he wanted to revoke Chen Defa's permit, Li replied that he had no right to revoke it. Chen Guansheng said that a deposit of 400 yuan was needed and he could handle it, so he borrowed 400 yuan from relatives and friends and handed it over to Chen Guansheng, but later realized he had been deceived. Next, witnesses Cai Guitang, Xia Liubao, Li Lianqi, and Xue Dezhang testified. Finally, the defendant Chen Guansheng testified that he had taken the 400 yuan, but because Mr. Wang refused to accept it, he returned it to Li Genfa, but Li wanted him to compensate for the loss and refused to accept it back. He had no choice but to take the money home, but it has now been taken away. The rest of his testimony was evasive. The judge ordered the defendant to be detained and remanded for further trial.

Promulgation of Children's Year Matters by the Chairman of the National Government; Ministries of Education, Interior, and Industry, together with the China Child Welfare Association, jointly organize the National Children's Year Implementation Committee.

The Shanghai China Child Welfare Association previously submitted a request to the National Government to stipulate and promulgate measures for Children's Year. The Executive Yuan instructed the Ministries of Education, Interior, and Industry to jointly draft Children's Year measures, which were subsequently passed by the 302nd and 206th meetings of the Executive Yuan and promulgated for nationwide implementation. Yesterday (the 22nd), the China Child Welfare Association received Official Letter No. 2095 from the Office of the Civil Affairs of the National Government, informing about various matters concerning Children's Year, including: "The implementation of Children's Year shall be presided over by the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Interior, and the Ministry of Industry, in conjunction with the China Child Welfare Association, to organize a National Children's Year Implementation Committee." The implementation procedures for the National Children's Year and the organizational regulations of the National Children's Year Implementation Committee as mentioned in the letter are hereby published as follows:

Implementation Procedures

The implementation procedures for the National Children's Year are as follows: "April of the 24th year" (1) Establish the National Children's Year Implementation Committee. Local Children's Year Implementation Committees shall be established uniformly by June 15th. (2) Begin composing songs for Children's Year "May of the same year." (3) Create various slogans and drawings for publicity. (4) Plan and edit small pamphlets on all matters concerning children's happiness for Children's Year. (5) Urge various provinces, cities, and counties to establish compulsory education committees to prepare for compulsory education, with the 24th year as the starting year for compulsory education. "June of the same year." (6) Compile and distribute activity outlines for various children's activities during Children's Year. (7) Formulate measures for holding various exhibitions during Children's Year. "July of the same year." (8) Formulate measures concerning the publication of special issues of newspapers and magazines during Children's Year, the publication of children's weekly magazines, and the writing of numerous essays on all matters concerning children's happiness, and request government orders for implementation. (9) Request the Central Radio Station to establish a lecture series on children's issues during Children's Year, broadcasting regular lectures on all matters concerning children. "August of the same year" (10) Hold the opening ceremony for Children's Year on the 1st (in collaboration with the Nanjing City Children's Year Implementation Committee). (11) Distribute publicity pamphlets on compulsory education. (12) Supervise various localities in establishing Mothers' Associations or Parents' Associations to teach methods of child rearing. (13) Establish children's problem consultation centers. "September of the same year" (14) Supervise various localities in holding children's speech contests. (15) Distribute publicity pamphlets on child-centered education. (16) Promote the abolition of corporal punishment in elementary schools and the release of all constraints on children. (17) Promote the establishment of child protection associations. "October of the same year" (18) Supervise various localities in holding children's recreational activities or sports meetings. (19) Distribute publicity pamphlets on children's civic training. (20) Research and formulate measures to advise on improving the treatment of child laborers and apprentices. (21) Supervise various localities in establishing children's amusement parks. "November of the same year" (22) Supervise various localities in establishing children's music societies. (23) Distribute pamphlets on "Instructions for Mothers" and "Instructions for Child Rearing." (24) Research and formulate appropriate educational measures for rescuing orphans, poor children, and disabled children. (25) Supervise the improvement of infant care institutions nationwide that lack scientific equipment and management. (26) Supervise local areas in establishing poor children's homes and orphan relief centers. "December of the same year" (27) Hold a national exhibition of children's reading materials. (28) Distribute publicity pamphlets on rescuing poor children. (29) Supervise various localities in establishing children's libraries. "January of the 25th year" (30) Supervise various localities in preparing for children's toy exhibitions. (31) Distribute publicity pamphlets on children's language education. (32) Research and formulate measures to prohibit harmful reading materials for children. "February of the same year" (33) Conduct a national compulsory education publicity week. (34) Distribute publicity pamphlets on rescuing out-of-school children. (35) Supervise elementary schools nationwide in implementing a two-part system to rescue out-of-school children. (36) Supervise various localities in establishing short-term elementary schools. (37) Supervise various localities in improving private schools. (38) Supervise various localities in carrying out universal smallpox vaccination for children. "March of the same year" (39) Supervise various localities in organizing children's afforestation teams. (40) Distribute publicity pamphlets guiding children in assisting construction. (41) Supervise various localities in holding children's art achievement exhibitions. "April of the same year" (42) Supervise various localities in holding expanded commemorative events and excursions for Children's Day. (43) Distribute publicity pamphlets on children's patriotic movements. (44) Hold a national children's toy exhibition. "May of the same year" (45) Encourage and guide children nationwide to use domestic goods. (46) Distribute publicity pamphlets on making and selecting children's toys. (47) Supervise various localities in holding children's health competitions. "June of the same year" (48) Supervise various localities in organizing children's hygiene teams. (49) Distribute publicity pamphlets on children's hygiene. (50) Supervise elementary schools nationwide in implementing hygiene implementation plans. (51) Supervise various localities in holding exhibitions of children's hygiene achievements. "July of the same year" (52) Encourage children nationwide to eliminate harmful birds and insects and protect beneficial birds and insects. (53) Guide various localities in organizing children's summer health camps. (54) Supervise various localities in establishing children's education centers. (55) Distribute publicity pamphlets on improving children's entrance examinations. (56) Hold the closing ceremony for Children's Year on the 21st. "August of the same year" (57) Investigate the implementation achievements of Children's Year in various localities. (58) All local Children's Year Implementation Committees shall be terminated. "September of the same year" (59) Compile all statistics regarding Children's Year. (60) Compile and print children's reports "October of the same year." (61) The National Children's Year Implementation Committee shall be completely terminated.

Organizational Regulations

The organizational regulations of the National Children's Year Implementation Committee are as follows: (Article 1) The National Children's Year Implementation Committee is organized in accordance with the provisions of Item 1 of the General Principles of the National Children's Year Implementation Law. (Article 2) This committee shall be composed of the following personnel: (1) The Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Interior shall each send three to five members. (2) The Ministry of Industry shall send two members. (3) The Ministry of Education, in conjunction with the Ministry of Interior, shall hire five to seven individuals with rich experience in children's education. (Article 3) The Ministry of Education, in conjunction with the Ministry of Interior, shall designate three members of the committee as standing committee members to handle routine matters. (Article 4) This committee shall hold a plenary meeting once a month and a standing committee meeting twice a month. (Article 5) This committee shall be responsible for guiding and supervising the implementation of Children's Year matters in various provinces, cities, and counties. (Article 7) This committee shall have one Director-General, appointed by the Ministry of Education in conjunction with the Ministry of Interior from among its staff members; five to nine staff members, appointed by the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Interior, and the Ministry of Industry from among their respective staff members. (Article 8) This committee may work in groups; the groups and their tasks shall be determined by the committee meeting. (Article 9) Members and staff of this committee shall be unpaid positions; however, members may be reimbursed for travel expenses incurred on official business, and staff may be given appropriate subsidies. (Article 10) The office of this committee shall be located within the Ministry of Education. (Article 11) This committee shall commence operations from April of the 24th year of the Republic of China and shall conclude in October of the 25th year. (Article 12) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Unprecedented Dense Fog in Shanghai Throughout Yesterday; Maritime Traffic Almost Blockaded; Aircraft Delayed, Then Returned.

Shanghai experienced an unprecedented heavy fog yesterday, with the weather being gloomy and dark throughout the day to an extreme degree. Air and sea transportation were both hindered. The various situations are recorded below:

Gloomy All Day

After 9 PM the night before, Shanghai experienced showers. Yesterday morning, the weather was still extremely cloudy. From 6 AM onwards, heavy fog suddenly descended, becoming increasingly dense. By 9 AM, it was difficult to distinguish faces even at close range. The atmospheric pressure dropped sharply, and the ground was extremely humid. Shops had to light lamps to operate, and offices indoors were the same. This type of fog did not dissipate until night.

Extremely Heavy Fog

The entire area of Pudong was shrouded in mist. Small ferries crossing the Huangpu River were threatened by the fog, appearing and disappearing vaguely, as if sailing in the clouds, creating a rather strange sight. At this time, not a single word could be seen on the customs' ship entry and exit boards, indicating that maritime traffic was completely blocked by the heavy fog.

Shipping Obstructed

As of yesterday evening, only a few ships had entered the port, including the Nagasaki Maru and Dalian Maru from overseas routes, and the Jiangtian, Ningshao, Gonghe, and Wusong from the Yangtze River route. Moreover, all were delayed due to the fog. Arrivals were between 3:30 PM and 5:10 PM. Many ships were blocked outside the port. For example, the Zhaoshangju's Haiyan vessel (coming from Hong Kong, expected to arrive in Shanghai at 2 PM) and the Xinming vessel (coming from Tianjin, also expected to arrive in Shanghai at 2 PM). For departures, apart from the Ningshao and Beijing vessels on the Shanghai-Ningbo line, which left port one after the other around 5 PM, it was uncertain whether the Zhaoshangju's Yushun, heading to Xiamen, and the Jiang'an, heading to the Yangtze River, could depart at night.

Aircraft Returns

According to China National Aviation Corporation, the westbound flight on the Shanghai-Hankou route was delayed from 7 AM to 11:10 AM before finally taking off, only to return at 11:40 AM and reschedule for today. The eastbound flight on the Shanghai-Hankou route arrived in Shanghai around 4 PM, also delayed by more than two hours.

Shenxin Textile Company Replies; Factories No. 2 and No. 5 Resume Operations as Ordered; Negotiations with Banking Syndicate for Further Loans.

After the Shenxin Textile Company's Factories No. 2 and No. 5 suspended operations, workers from both factories petitioned party and government authorities, requesting that the factory be ordered to resume operations as soon as possible to maintain the livelihoods of the workers. Now, the Social Affairs Bureau has received an order from the Municipal Government instructing the company to find ways to resume operations immediately. It is reported that the company has been negotiating with a banking syndicate composed of banks such as the Bank of China and the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank for further loans to facilitate an early resumption of operations, and this has become concrete. Therefore, Rong Zongjing, the general manager of the company, has replied to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, stating that he will comply with the order to find ways to resume operations.

Shanghai Gas Company to Voluntarily Reduce Prices Starting Next Month.

The Shanghai Gas Company has recently adopted a new gas manufacturing method, resulting in lower costs. Furthermore, in order to promote users, it is reported that it has decided to voluntarily implement price reductions starting on May 1st. For example, the previous charge of $2.85 per thousand cubic feet will be reduced to $2.25, a reduction of about 21%. If consumption is below 900 cubic feet, the charge will be only $2.50. Other fees, such as meter installation, will also be slightly reduced.

Publication of the Third Series of "Siming Series" Adds Splendor to Literature.

The "Siming Series," edited by Zhang Shouyong, the owner of Yueyuan, has been widely praised by the literary community since the publication of its first and second series. The secret editions collected are mostly unseen by the world. Therefore, not only are people in our country vying to purchase and read them, but libraries around the world are also continuously sending letters and telegrams to order them. This time, to meet the needs of all parties, in addition to reprinting 1,000 copies each of the first and second series, the third series is scheduled to be published at the end of June. In the first series, there are Song Chunqiu Jishi, 4 volumes; Song Shihao, Book of Documents Lectures, 20 volumes; Song Lou Yi, Fan Wenzheng Gong Chronological Biography, 1 volume, Sleeve Relics, 1 volume; Song Yang Jian, Cihu Poetry Biography, 20 volumes, Appendix, 1 volume; Six Volumes of Great Teachings of the Early Sages; Song Gui Wanrong, Comparison of Cases of Tang Yin, 1 volume; Song Que Yue Ling Jie, 12 volumes; Song Wei Xian, Siming Tasanshui Water Conservancy Overview, 6 volumes; Gou Xu, Collation Notes, 1 volume; Song Yuan Fu, Meng Zhong Dian Lecture Notes, 4 volumes; Yuan Shu, Six Familiar Outlines of People, 2 volumes, Appendix, 1 volume; Zhang Yong, Compiling Collation Records, 1 volume; Ming Dao Si Dao, Spring Grass Collection, 1 volume; Ming Huang Runyu, Ningbo Prefecture Concise Records, 5 volumes; Hai Han Wan Xianglu, 4 volumes; Ming Dong Shou, On Reading Yi, 1 volume, Notes on Yi, 4 volumes; Qing Wan Sitong, Confucian School Factions, 16 volumes; Qing Jiang Xueyong, Yin Drafts, 4 volumes; Qing Zhou Daozun, Yongshang Water Conservancy Records, 6 volumes. A total of 17 kinds, 181 volumes, are all valuable rare books. Among them, Zhang's Six Arts Collation Notes and Zhang's late father Xiao Gong's handwritten copy are especially precious. The price is 90 yuan per set. Those who pre-order before June can get a 20% discount. The sales address is No. 11 Jueyuan, Avenue Edward VII, Shanghai.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Urges All Industries to Expedite Fundraising for the Wusong Dredging Project.

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent letters to 25 trade associations, including the Northern Goods Industry, Flour Mill Industry, Native Goods Industry, Sugar Industry, and Fresh Fish Industry, stating: "We are writing to you regarding the matter of collecting funds from various industries for the Wusong dredging project, as instructed by the Municipal Government. Two fundraising methods have been proposed: (1) donating a certain amount; (2) collecting a certain amount per unit of goods. We have sent these methods to the relevant industries, asking you to choose one of the two and do your best to raise funds. We have repeatedly sent letters urging those who have not yet responded or have responded but not yet taken action. Now, we find that the amount of funds that various industries have paid or pledged for this project is still far short of the 150,000 yuan agreed upon with the Municipal Government. We have repeatedly reported the difficulties of various industries to the Municipal Government, and we have twice received replies from the Municipal Government urging us to do our best and not to refuse. Judging from the wording of the replies, since the section undertaken by the provincial authorities has already started construction, there is no reason to allow the section dredged by this city to be interrupted. Therefore, the Chamber of Commerce cannot simply relay empty words in this matter. Various industries should do their best to raise funds in the hope of seeing the project completed soon. We are sending another letter urging you to discuss and implement this matter quickly, and to promptly reply to the Chamber of Commerce with the amount pledged. Do not delay. This is our earnest hope."

Hu Maojing, Manager of Xingguang Daily, Comes to Shanghai to Investigate the Newspaper Industry; Simultaneously Purchasing New Rotary Printing Press.

Hu Maojing, the general manager of the Xiamen Xingguang Daily, recently came to Shanghai on the Dutch postal ship Zibaide to prepare for the newspaper's publication. This reporter met him at the New Shanghai Hotel yesterday and inquired about the purpose of his visit. According to him, the overseas Chinese tycoon Hu Wenhu is very enthusiastic about promoting the newspaper industry. The Xingzhou Daily, which he founded in Singapore in Southeast Asia, is the center of public opinion for the overseas Chinese and holds the authority of the local newspaper industry, which is already known to everyone. After the Min Guo Daily closed down, Hu also purchased its printing press, fonts, etc., to publish the Xingwu Daily. At the same time, he founded the Xinyue and Xingguang newspapers in Guangzhou and Xiamen in China, actively proceeding with all his strength. The site of the Xinyue Daily is under construction, and the Xingguang Daily has purchased a five-story building on Zhongshan Road in Xiamen, and is currently engaged in internal installation. I (Hu referred to himself) came to Shanghai to investigate everything to learn from it, since our newspaper is about to be published and Shanghai is the center of our country's news and cultural industry. I also came to purchase the latest rotary printing press, typecasting machines, copper molds, etc. Yesterday, I was led by Hu Guigeng and Lang Jingshan to visit major newspapers and visit celebrities in the news industry. I will stay in Shanghai for a few more days before returning to Xiamen to prepare for publication.

Judging from the spirit of handling this picnic, it is possible to deduce a general idea.

Maid Beaten to Death; Husband Comes to Shanghai to Sue; Case Has Been Heard and Awaits Judgment.

Lin, a rural woman from Hefei, Anhui, who was 45 years old, was working as a maid in Shanghai. On the evening of March 1st, in front of No. 137 Rue Paul Beau in the French Concession, she was beaten by hooligans Fei Jinhai (nicknamed "Little Rice Cake") and Zhang Xiaomao due to a dispute over pouring sewage. She died the next morning. The French Concession police arrested the two murderers one after another and sent them to the Special First Court for trial. On the 9th of this month, Fei was sentenced to 12 years in prison and Zhang to 7 years, with their civil rights revoked for the same period as their sentences. Later, the deceased's husband, Ni Jishi, received the news in his hometown and came to Shanghai. According to the information provided by his fellow villagers Wang Benyin, Xu Shaoqing, the deceased's little sister Han Sijie, and Sister Wang, namely Chen Wangshi, the death of his wife Lin was actually instigated by Wang Yongwen, the owner of Shunxing Water and Electricity Materials Company at No. 137 Rue Paul Beau, and Chen Guanghan, the owner of Chen Yuanmao Restaurant at No. 135 next door, who colluded with the already arrested and punished Little Rice Cake and Zhang Xiaomao, and the fugitive Little Amei, Bao San, Liang Du, A Xing, and others to beat her to death. Furthermore, the employer Chen Li's family failed to pay wages at the time of her injuries and sent her to the hospital for treatment, which also involved dereliction of duty. Ni hired a lawyer to file a private prosecution with the Criminal Division of the Special Second Court against the above seven people for instigating injury, abandonment, and causing death, requesting legal investigation and punishment. He also filed a civil lawsuit, jointly seeking damages and compensation for wages of $950 and funeral expenses of $500, totaling $1,450, from Fei and Zhang, who had already been prosecuted and sentenced, and all the defendants in the private prosecution. The Special Second Court's Judge Zhang Chaozuo opened a court hearing and summoned all parties, as detailed in this newspaper. The day before yesterday, the court hearing continued. The plaintiff was still accompanied by his lawyer and the witnesses Wang Benyin, Xu Shaoqing, Han Sijie, and Sister Wang. Of the defendants, Little Amei, Bao San, Liang Du, etc. of No. 1, 2, and 3, etc., were still untraceable, and the summons could not be served. The others, such as A Xing (11 years old, surname Zhang), Wang Yongwen, Chen Guanghan, and Chen Li (employer), etc., appeared in court in response to the summons. The judge briefly questioned both parties and the witnesses, and then summoned the witness, Officer Tian Shiqing, No. 58, of the French Concession Police, who was in charge of the case, to provide testimony. He testified that on the morning of March 2, a resident of the Chungui Lane in Bedier Road came to the police station to report that a corpse had been found abandoned in the lane. I immediately went to investigate with a western detective and saw that the corpse was covered with straw mats. Upon uncovering, the deceased had injuries to the back of the head, and there was blood on the back of her clothes. After repeated inquiries, it was learned that the body had been moved out from the Fangji Introduction Shop next door. I immediately inquired with the shop, and they said that she had been hit and killed by a car. After further investigation, it was learned that her employer and the two women who testified (referring to Han Sijie and Sister Wang) initially said that she had been hit by a car as well. However, since the injuries did not seem to be caused by a car, it was determined that she had been beaten. Then, the two women revealed that she had been beaten and pointed out the murderers Little Rice Cake, Zhang Xiaomao, and Shi Bao San, etc. The women in the introduction shop who moved the body, Fang Lin's family and Luo Geng's family, were also detained. Later, the murderers were apprehended. After investigation, since there was no evidence against Shi Bao San, he was released. The murderers Fei and Zhang, and the Lin and Geng families were sent to the court for trial. Initially, no one reported that the defendants in the case were at the scene instigating and helping the crime. The judge then ordered Tian to file the testimony for the record, and then ordered the attorneys to make their arguments. The court then adjourned the hearing and announced that the judgment would be pronounced at a later date. The defendants left to await the announcement.

A Man Murdered on Fulvli Road: Three Axe Wounds to the Back of His Head Shatter His Skull

At around 9:00 PM last night, a man, approximately thirty years old, was found lying seriously injured by the roadside in front of No. 284 Fulvli Road in the French Concession. He had been attacked with an axe by an enemy. He was wearing a blue cloth long gown over a white cloth shirt and trousers. Someone immediately reported the incident to the nearby police, who in turn reported it to the police station. The police chief immediately dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to investigate. They found the man lying on his back in a pool of blood, covered in blood stains. He had three axe wounds to the back of his head, and his skull was shattered. He was already unconscious. He was rushed to the Guangci Hospital on Jin Shenfu Road for treatment, but due to the severity of his injuries, he died within half an hour of arriving at the hospital. The hospital notified the police station, which in turn notified the Tongren Fuyuan branch. The branch ordered undertakers to transport the body to the coroner's office, awaiting an examination by the Second Special District Court today. Meanwhile, the police station notified all detectives to arrest the perpetrator and investigate the matter.

Central Bank Inspection Report No. 230

Central Bank Issuance Reserve 230th Inspection Report states, This committee, in accordance with the current provisions of Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the Bank's issuance of convertible notes. The 230th inspection was held at the Bank's Issuance Bureau on April 10th, 24th year of the Republic of China. The inspection results are hereby announced as follows, (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued is 91,149,127 silver dollars, including 84,191,965 silver dollar notes and 6,957,162 auxiliary coin notes. The total amount of convertible note reserves is 91,149,127 silver dollars, including 72,369,127 silver dollars in cash reserves. Of this cash reserve, 68,510,366 yuan is stored in the Bank's Issuance Depository, 2,042,230 yuan is stored in branch offices in various cities, and 1,816,531 yuan is stored with fellow institutions. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 18,780,000 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued is 373,324.7 customs gold units. The total amount of customs gold convertible note reserves is 373,324.7 customs gold units. This reserve includes 7,351 taels, 9 mace and 5 fen of standard gold, which is equivalent to 373,324.7 customs gold units at a fixed price of 0.50779. According to Article 1 of the Central Bank's convertible note regulations, 60% of the reserve should be in cash and 40% in guarantee. The results of this inspection show that the cash portion exceeds 60% and the guarantee portion is less than 40%, which is consistent with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. April 22, 24th year of the Republic of China. Li Fusun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Supervisors Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilao.

Li Jingzhai, an expert in abdominal distension from Yuyao, possesses a secret ancestral formula that specializes in treating all types of fluid accumulation, gas accumulation, and menstrual swelling in women. City News

Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Lines Offer Preferential Treatment to Members of the Road Association. The China National Road Construction Association, in order to facilitate travel for its members, sent letters to hotels in various locations a month ago, requesting them to offer special treatment and reduce room rates for its members. The hotels, recognizing the large number of association members, were happy to offer special discounts in addition to the actual room rates, ranging from 60% to 90%, to show their goodwill. All members of the association who hold a membership card and stay at the hotels agreed upon by the association can enjoy this special privilege. The names of the agreed-upon hotels on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou railway lines are listed below: (Nanjing) Anle Hotel, Oriental Hotel; (Wuxi) Taihu Hotel, Railway Hotel, Jiaotong Inn, New World Inn; (Suzhou) Railway Hotel; (Hangzhou) Xiling Hotel, Hubin Inn, Xintai Inn, Qingtai Di Inn, Southeast Hotel, Shenghu Inn. It is reported that there are also other hotels in various locations that have been agreed upon, which are detailed in the March issue of the association's Road Monthly. Members who wish to travel can call the association for inquiries.

The sound is clear, the style is beautiful, and it is easy to carry, making it a good companion for travel. It is reported that the price of each radio is only 42 yuan, and the shipping fee for out-of-town purchases is an additional 1 yuan.

After decades of hard work, it has become a leader in China's food industry. At a time when the world is experiencing a commercial depression, Mr. Xi Guansheng, a giant in the food industry, has the spirit of an iron army. The company was able to purchase land in Caohejing, Xuhui, and open a farm, and build a new four-story steel and concrete factory, which is evident to all. At the shareholders' meeting on the 24th of last month, it was decided to increase the share capital by 200,000 yuan. Since this news was released, it has been extremely welcomed by all sectors, and there is a rush to subscribe. It is reported that more than 100,000 yuan has already been subscribed by new and old shareholders yesterday, and it is likely to exceed the quota. This is also a positive phenomenon in China's food industry.

Weather Report

Xujiahui Observatory: The weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong Province and surrounding areas are cloudy with northeasterly winds. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy with fog or rain, and the wind is from the southeast to northeast. The East China Sea and the Ryukyu Islands have cyclones and rain due to the passage of a small low-pressure center moving towards the east-northeast. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 67.1 degrees and the lowest was 57.7 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 68.5 degrees and the lowest was 55.8 degrees.

Education News

The First Day of the Municipal Normal School Examination: Director Pan Personally Inspects, Orderly Conditions in All Examination Halls

The municipal government's 23rd annual second semester normal school graduate examination commenced yesterday at Shangwen, Xicheng, and Wuben. More than 500 students participated. Each examination hall had two chief examiners and four mutual examiners. Candidates from each school were accompanied by school staff who arrived at the examination halls on time. Candidate admission tickets were checked at the entrance, and student seating arrangements were pre-arranged by the Bureau of Education. Director Pan personally visited and inspected each examination hall yesterday and offered instructions. Conditions in the examination halls were quite good. All examination papers were sealed, opened on the spot by the chief examiners, and distributed according to number. After the examination was completed, the examination papers were collected, sealed by the chief examiners, stamped with their personal seals, and returned to the Bureau of Education to be reviewed and graded by the examination committee. The committee then unsealed the papers to verify the names and marks. The process was quite strict. Today's examination subjects in the morning for each group are arithmetic and party principles, and in the afternoon for each group are history and geography.

The Final Day of the Reading Movement: Director Pan Broadcasts Closing Remarks, The Purpose of the Reading Movement is to Build a New China, the Reading Movement Should Expand Space and Extend Time

Yesterday was the final day of the National Reading Movement Conference organized by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association. Director Pan Gongzhan, Secretary-General of the Association, broadcast the closing remarks of the National Reading Movement Conference from the China-West Radio Station. The Association has been inviting scholars and celebrities to give academic system broadcasts and lectures for days, which has attracted much attention and welcome from the academic community. The Association plans to ask the speakers to supplement and revise the recorded manuscripts and publish them in the Cultural Construction Monthly to meet the needs of readers nationwide. The full text of Pan's closing remarks is as follows: Gentlemen, today is the last day of the National Reading Movement Conference organized by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association. I am responsible for giving the closing remarks. The Reading Movement Conference has now officially concluded, but the Reading Movement will definitely not end with the closing of the conference. This point should be noted by our compatriots throughout the country.

Regarding the significance of this National Reading Movement Conference organized by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association, Mr. Chen Lifu, Chairman of the Association, gave a detailed report on "National Revival and Reading Movement" in Nanjing on the Central Broadcasting Station. The speech has been published in major newspapers across the country, and I need not repeat it. The "Relationship between Cultural Construction and Reading Movement" was also discussed in detail by Mr. Wu Tiecheng, Vice-Chairman of the Association, on April 15. The connection between the Reading Movement and the Chinese Revolution was also discussed with you by Mr. Wu Xingya, Standing Director of the Association, on April 8. As for the methods of reading, the attitude that should be taken in researching various academic disciplines, and the methods that should be adopted, succinct instructions were given by academic celebrities such as Cai Yuanpei and Wang Yunwu. The original texts of the speeches have been published in major newspapers. After young people across the country have heard or read the famous sayings and theories of these gentlemen, I deeply believe that those who have no interest in reading will definitely be inspired to make a determined effort to study academic disciplines, and those who have an interest in reading will definitely be able to strengthen their confidence in academic research. Therefore, the significance of the Reading Movement Conference lies in arousing the determination and confidence of young people across the country in reading, and in arousing a firm motive for reading. Therefore, although the conference ended according to the scheduled date, I deeply believe that the interest of our compatriots across the country in reading and the determination to study academic disciplines will be stimulated and become more determined as a result of the closing of the conference. Now, I would like to offer some opinions on the Reading Movement, hoping that young people across the country will pay attention and all sectors of society will give guidance. We all feel that the Chinese nation has reached a critical moment of life and death. Whether we can recover from this crisis depends entirely on whether we are able to diagnose and treat the Chinese patient correctly and whether we are able to recuperate appropriately. Assuming that we can diagnose and treat the patient properly and recuperate appropriately, then the patient will undoubtedly recover. Perhaps we will be even stronger than before. Assuming that the diagnosis, treatment, and recuperation are not appropriate, it is possible that the disease will become critical and lead to death. Post-revolutionary China is like a pregnant woman giving birth. The difficulty and hardship of the revolution and its impact on the social, political, and economic aspects of the country are far greater than the difficulty of childbirth for a pregnant woman. Post-revolutionary China is also like the weak body of a pregnant woman after childbirth, which is in a very dangerous period. The death of a pregnant woman is often due to improper postpartum care. There are two major stages of revolution: destruction and construction. Destruction is analogous to childbirth for a pregnant woman, and construction is analogous to postpartum care. We have initiated the revolution in order to accelerate the progress of society, politics, and economy. This revolutionary movement has destroyed all outdated and corrupt social, political, and economic systems. After that, we must build a sound and rational social, political, and economic system. Assuming that there is only destruction and no construction, it is like a pregnant woman who only knows how to give birth but does not know how to take care of herself, who only knows how to give birth but does not know how to raise her child. If a pregnant woman gives birth but does not know how to take care of herself and raise her child, both the mother and the child will be in danger. If we only know how to revolt but do not know how to build, not only will the revolution fail, but there will also be the disaster of national subjugation and racial extinction. Therefore, in the current stage of China, the work of destruction has been largely completed. Today, the only thing needed is a vigorous construction movement. When it comes to construction, we need construction materials, construction personnel, and construction methods. Without construction materials, personnel, and methods, how can construction be completed? Construction materials need to be obtained by specialists and technicians. Construction personnel need to be trained by specialists and technicians. We need intelligence. Despite having five-year plans and ten-year plans, if there are no construction materials and personnel, it is still just empty talk. The need for intelligence is so urgent, then cultivating intelligence and enriching intelligence is of course the only urgent task today. From this, we can see the urgency and need for the Reading Movement in the current stage of the Chinese Revolution. Therefore, the current Chinese Reading Movement is a construction-oriented Reading Movement. It is a Reading Movement that aims to build a new China. If young people still only know how to destroy but do not know how to build, just like pregnant women who only know how to give birth but do not know how to take care of themselves, who only know how to give birth but do not know how to raise their children, then it is equally dangerous. Not only will young people themselves go astray and ruin their lives, but the nation will also suffer a major blow. The entire revolutionary movement will inevitably lead to failure. The Reading Movement at the current stage is a construction-oriented Reading Movement. This is the first point that I hope everyone will deeply understand and pay serious attention to. Secondly, what I just said seems to focus more on specialized research. On the one hand, we need to cultivate many experts to build a new China. This refers to the general youth who have received education or are receiving education, and train themselves to become leading personnel in building a new China. This is of course what China urgently needs. However, while cultivating specialized talents, we cannot ignore the majority of the ignorant and illiterate. Assuming that China's vast illiterate population is not eliminated and more than 80% of the people do not have the opportunity to receive education, then China's revolution will still not be completed, and China's construction cause will still be hampered by many obstacles. Our country has 470 million compatriots. Even if we say that China's illiterate population is less than 80%, it is at least 70%. Even with 70%, there are 329 million illiterate people who are excluded from the circle of knowledge. How can China's construction cause be completed if this vast illiterate population is abandoned? For example, in architecture, if the foundation is not strong, the achievement will be small. Therefore, on the one hand, we must cultivate many young people who are in school and who have received education to become specialists. At the same time, we must eliminate China's vast illiterate population. I firmly believe that among this vast illiterate population, once they have received literacy education, there will definitely be many outstanding talents who can be discovered and serve the people and the country. Now, the central government and the provincial and municipal governments are all committed to eliminating the literacy movement. I hope that all members of the Chinese Cultural Construction Association and comrades across the country will participate in this great movement to eliminate illiteracy. We must know that eliminating illiteracy is also the second key point of our Reading Movement. Thirdly, what I mentioned earlier is that the purpose of the Reading Movement is construction, and the second point is that the Reading Movement should eliminate illiteracy and expand space. The third point is that the Reading Movement should extend the time and have permanence. As I said earlier, the significance of the Reading Movement Conference lies in arousing the public's motivation and interest in reading, and in awakening the public to the importance of reading in the current stage of the Chinese Revolution. Therefore, after the motivation and interest have been aroused and the importance of the Reading Movement has been understood, although the conference has ended, we should develop a good and lasting habit of reading, which is an important task. The four basic needs of life are clothing, food, shelter, and transportation. I hope that in the future, it can become clothing, food, shelter, transportation, and reading, and regard reading as an indispensable daily necessity of life, just like clothing, food, shelter, and transportation. No matter how busy a person is at work, they should set aside one hour, two hours, or three hours a day to read. Young people who are in school should especially strive to work hard and study diligently, and be determined to create themselves into important leading personnel for building a new China. The Reading Movement should be a lasting movement, and reading should become one of the daily needs of every citizen. This is the third key point of the Reading Movement. After many gentlemen have troubled themselves to give us many instructions on the methods and attitudes of studying academic disciplines, I offer the above three points of view on the day of the closing of the conference, hoping that comrades across the country will deeply understand, put them into practice, and give corrections. The end.

Secondary School Normal Education Association: The Examination Group Holds Research Meeting Yesterday, Advocates Abolishing School Graduation Examinations, The Training and Military Training Group to Hold Research Meeting Today

The Municipal Secondary School Normal Education Research Association commenced its group research meetings yesterday at the YMCA in Ba Xian Qiao. The first day was for the Graduation Examination Group, and today is for the Training and Military Training Group. Details are as follows:

Examination Group: The Graduation Examination Group met on the third floor of the YMCA in Ba Xian Qiao at 1:00 PM yesterday. Attending members included Chen Jicheng, Tao Guangchuan, Tao Zailiang, Lu Shiyin, Wu Youxiao, Yang Daohong, Shen Tilan, Zhang Jiashu, Ji Haopei, Lu Xirong, Xu Renhan, Feng Yixian, Tang Naikang, and others. Zeng Kewei, Qian Fugong, and Zhang Zhu from the Bureau of Education also attended. Chairman Chen Jicheng, Recording Secretary Wu Youxiao. Research questions: (1) Should school graduation examinations be abolished? Resolved: They should be abolished. (2) If high school students who fail one or two subjects in the first or second semester fail the supplementary examination twice, but have been promoted to colleges or universities on a trial basis, how should the issue of their student status be resolved? Resolved: If their performance on the trial basis is excellent, their student status should be recognized and they do not need to retake the courses. The colleges and universities should formulate their own methods. (3) Should normal school graduates who fail one or two subjects on the graduation examination be allowed to serve temporarily? Resolved: They should be allowed to serve temporarily, but they should not be allowed to teach the subjects they failed. There should also be a distinction in terms of employment and treatment between them and students who pass all subjects. The Bureau of Education should formulate its own regulations. (4) Should the method of calculating and disclosing the standard of the school graduation examination results be changed? Resolved: To be reserved for discussion at the next meeting. (5) The above cases are designated for discussion by the Ministry of Education. Next, impromptu motions: 1. Shen Tilan proposed the fundamental abolition of the graduation examination. Resolved: To be reserved for discussion at the next meeting. 2. Date of the next meeting. Resolved: To be held at 2:00 PM next Monday, still at the YMCA in Ba Xian Qiao.

Training Group: The Training and Military Training Group will hold its first research meeting at 1:00 PM this afternoon in the meeting room on the third floor of the YMCA in Ba Xian Qiao. Discussion questions: (1) Opinions on formulating the content of the training standard; (2) How to make school training permeate the actual lives of every student; (3) What are the difficulties in student management after the implementation of centralized military training; (4) Suggestions on the implementation methods of military management. Members Lin Meiyan, Tong Xingbai, Jia Guanren, Shen Weizhen, Chen Bangyan, Zhang Shilin, Chen Mengyu, Tao Zailiang, Wang Jinyun, Guo Shouchun, Tang Zengyang, Huang Yiru, and others.

Tai Shuangqiu Speaks on People's Livelihood Education

This semester, Great China University in this city has established a lecture series on national salvation, inviting celebrities to give lectures from time to time. The other day, the university invited He Shuangqiu, the dean of the School of Education, to speak on people's livelihood education. The gist of Tai's speech was that the fundamental problem in China is the problem of people's livelihood. The current rural education, mass education, and production education in China all fail to emphasize people's livelihood. Therefore, he advocated promoting people's livelihood-based education (in short, people's livelihood education) with the development of people's economic activities as the backbone, to improve people's lives, support social survival, protect the lives of the masses, and achieve the goal of people's prosperity and recovery. As for the method of solving the problem of people's livelihood, Tai advocated using industry to enrich agriculture, integrating industry into agriculture, maintaining the inherent manual production, improving it, and gradually developing it into cooperative small-scale machine crafts, spreading them in China's rural areas. Finally, Tai also said that if we want to help the countryside, the fundamental plan is to promote the use of local products produced in the countryside, especially hand-spun and hand-woven local cloth. Local products should enter the city, not national products go to the countryside. Entrepreneurs should go to the countryside to promote cooperative crafts, and should not suck the money from the countryside into the city to open factories, making rural finance exhausted. He's discussion was eloquent and thorough, and the audience applauded thunderously. It is heard that Great China University and the Recitation Movement Promotion Association have a people's livelihood education experimental area in Fanwangdu in this city, using the Recitation Society's method for experimentation. He's advocacy has been for many years, and he welcomes all parties to visit and participate.

Central Party Headquarters Basketball Team First Victory Over East Asia Yesterday; Result 24 to 16; Tonight at 7 PM Fight Against Youyou

Jiangda Volleyball Order; Games Begin on the 30th of This Month

The competition rules and order of this year's Jiangda volleyball competition have been decided by the committee and announced as follows:

(1) The competition adopts a knockout system.

(2) The competition rules shall be implemented in accordance with the latest published volleyball rules of the National Sports Federation.

(3) The referees shall be hired by the host team with the consent of the visiting team, or the host team shall request the Chinese Referees Association to appoint them.

(4) In case of rain, the host team shall try to borrow the gymnasium to hold the event and shall not postpone it.

(3) The registration form must be submitted to the chairman of the ranking committee (Zheng Bingde, Fudan University) no later than one day before the competition.

(6) The location and referees of the finals shall be decided and hired by the committee.

(7) The competition time is from 2:00 PM for women and 3:00 PM for men.

Four World Records

(Brunswick, 20th Reuters) American swimmer Hitchens today created a world record in the 100-meter breaststroke with a time of 7 minutes and 27 seconds, far exceeding the old record of 7 minutes and 33.1 seconds set by Germany's Schwarz.
